select  distinct z.numfactu, b.fechafac,convert(varchar(10), cast(b.fechafac as date), 101) fecha,nombres,
 (
 select  sum(a.cantidad*a.precunit) 
 from cma_DFactura a 
 where z.numfactu=a.numfactu
 ) subtotal,
 (
 select  sum(descuento)
 from cma_DFactura a 
 where z.numfactu=a.numfactu
 ) descuento,

 (
 select  (sum(a.cantidad*a.precunit) -sum(descuento))
 from cma_DFactura a 
 where z.numfactu=a.numfactu
 ) total

 from cma_DFactura z
 inner join cma_MFactura b On z.numfactu=b.numfactu  
 inner join MInventario c On c.coditems=z.coditems
 inner join MClientes d On d.codclien=b.codclien   
 where b.fechafac between   '01/01/2019' and '09/03/2019'  and b.statfact=3  AND b.codmedico='333' and z.coditems  not in ( 'CMKCINTRON','CMKCINT1CO','CMKCINTSEG' ,'0000000000')

union all

  select  distinct z.numnotcre, b.fechanot,convert(varchar(10), cast(b.fechanot as date), 101) fecha,nombres,
 (
 select  sum(a.cantidad*a.precunit) *-1
 from CMA_Dnotacredito a 
 where z.numnotcre=a.numnotcre
 ) subtotal,
 (
 select  sum(descuento) *-1
 from CMA_Dnotacredito a 
 where z.numnotcre=a.numnotcre 
 ) descuento,

 (
 select  (sum(a.cantidad*a.precunit) -sum(descuento)) *-1
 from CMA_Dnotacredito a 
 where z.numnotcre=a.numnotcre
 ) total

 from CMA_Dnotacredito z
 inner join CMA_Mnotacredito b On z.numnotcre=b.numnotcre
 inner join MInventario c On c.coditems=z.coditems
 inner join MClientes d On d.codclien=b.codclien   
 where b.fechanot between  '01/01/2019' and '09/03/2019'  and b.statnc=3  AND b.codmedico='333' and z.coditems  not in ( 'CMKCINTRON','CMKCINT1CO','CMKCINTSEG' ,'0000000000')
 order by numfactu desc

[2019-09-03 20:30:19.000000 192.130.75.223  - [query->JOLALDE] ] 
select  distinct z.numfactu, b.fechafac,convert(varchar(10), cast(b.fechafac as date), 101) fecha,nombres,
 (
 select  sum(a.cantidad*a.precunit) 
 from cma_DFactura a 
 where z.numfactu=a.numfactu
 ) subtotal,
 (
 select  sum(descuento)
 from cma_DFactura a 
 where z.numfactu=a.numfactu
 ) descuento,

 (
 select  (sum(a.cantidad*a.precunit) -sum(descuento))
 from cma_DFactura a 
 where z.numfactu=a.numfactu
 ) total

 from cma_DFactura z
 inner join cma_MFactura b On z.numfactu=b.numfactu  
 inner join MInventario c On c.coditems=z.coditems
 inner join MClientes d On d.codclien=b.codclien   
 where b.fechafac between   '01/01/2019' and '09/03/2019'  and b.statfact=3  AND b.codmedico='333' and z.coditems  not in ( 'CMKCINTRON','CMKCINT1CO','CMKCINTSEG' ,'0000000000')

union all

  select  distinct z.numnotcre, b.fechanot,convert(varchar(10), cast(b.fechanot as date), 101) fecha,nombres,
 (
 select  sum(a.cantidad*a.precunit) *-1
 from CMA_Dnotacredito a 
 where z.numnotcre=a.numnotcre
 ) subtotal,
 (
 select  sum(descuento) *-1
 from CMA_Dnotacredito a 
 where z.numnotcre=a.numnotcre 
 ) descuento,

 (
 select  (sum(a.cantidad*a.precunit) -sum(descuento)) *-1
 from CMA_Dnotacredito a 
 where z.numnotcre=a.numnotcre
 ) total

 from CMA_Dnotacredito z
 inner join CMA_Mnotacredito b On z.numnotcre=b.numnotcre
 inner join MInventario c On c.coditems=z.coditems
 inner join MClientes d On d.codclien=b.codclien   
 where b.fechanot between  '01/01/2019' and '09/03/2019'  and b.statnc=3  AND b.codmedico='333' and z.coditems  not in ( 'CMKCINTRON','CMKCINT1CO','CMKCINTSEG' ,'0000000000')
 order by numfactu desc

select  distinct z.numfactu, b.fechafac,convert(varchar(10), cast(b.fechafac as date), 101) fecha,nombres,
 (
 select  sum(a.cantidad*a.precunit) 
 from cma_DFactura a 
 where z.numfactu=a.numfactu
 ) subtotal,
 (
 select  sum(descuento)
 from cma_DFactura a 
 where z.numfactu=a.numfactu
 ) descuento,

 (
 select  (sum(a.cantidad*a.precunit) -sum(descuento))
 from cma_DFactura a 
 where z.numfactu=a.numfactu
 ) total

 from cma_DFactura z
 inner join cma_MFactura b On z.numfactu=b.numfactu  
 inner join MInventario c On c.coditems=z.coditems
 inner join MClientes d On d.codclien=b.codclien   
 where b.fechafac between   '06/02/2019' and '09/03/2019'  and b.statfact=3  AND b.codmedico='333' and z.coditems  not in ( 'CMKCINTRON','CMKCINT1CO','CMKCINTSEG' ,'0000000000')

union all

  select  distinct z.numnotcre, b.fechanot,convert(varchar(10), cast(b.fechanot as date), 101) fecha,nombres,
 (
 select  sum(a.cantidad*a.precunit) *-1
 from CMA_Dnotacredito a 
 where z.numnotcre=a.numnotcre
 ) subtotal,
 (
 select  sum(descuento) *-1
 from CMA_Dnotacredito a 
 where z.numnotcre=a.numnotcre 
 ) descuento,

 (
 select  (sum(a.cantidad*a.precunit) -sum(descuento)) *-1
 from CMA_Dnotacredito a 
 where z.numnotcre=a.numnotcre
 ) total

 from CMA_Dnotacredito z
 inner join CMA_Mnotacredito b On z.numnotcre=b.numnotcre
 inner join MInventario c On c.coditems=z.coditems
 inner join MClientes d On d.codclien=b.codclien   
 where b.fechanot between  '06/02/2019' and '09/03/2019'  and b.statnc=3  AND b.codmedico='333' and z.coditems  not in ( 'CMKCINTRON','CMKCINT1CO','CMKCINTSEG' ,'0000000000')
 order by numfactu desc

select  distinct z.numfactu, b.fechafac,convert(varchar(10), cast(b.fechafac as date), 101) fecha,nombres,
 (
 select  sum(a.cantidad*a.precunit) 
 from cma_DFactura a 
 where z.numfactu=a.numfactu
 ) subtotal,
 (
 select  sum(descuento)
 from cma_DFactura a 
 where z.numfactu=a.numfactu
 ) descuento,

 (
 select  (sum(a.cantidad*a.precunit) -sum(descuento))
 from cma_DFactura a 
 where z.numfactu=a.numfactu
 ) total

 from cma_DFactura z
 inner join cma_MFactura b On z.numfactu=b.numfactu  
 inner join MInventario c On c.coditems=z.coditems
 inner join MClientes d On d.codclien=b.codclien   
 where b.fechafac between   '09/01/2019' and '09/03/2019'  and b.statfact=3  AND b.codmedico='333' and z.coditems  not in ( 'CMKCINTRON','CMKCINT1CO','CMKCINTSEG' ,'0000000000')

union all

  select  distinct z.numnotcre, b.fechanot,convert(varchar(10), cast(b.fechanot as date), 101) fecha,nombres,
 (
 select  sum(a.cantidad*a.precunit) *-1
 from CMA_Dnotacredito a 
 where z.numnotcre=a.numnotcre
 ) subtotal,
 (
 select  sum(descuento) *-1
 from CMA_Dnotacredito a 
 where z.numnotcre=a.numnotcre 
 ) descuento,

 (
 select  (sum(a.cantidad*a.precunit) -sum(descuento)) *-1
 from CMA_Dnotacredito a 
 where z.numnotcre=a.numnotcre
 ) total

 from CMA_Dnotacredito z
 inner join CMA_Mnotacredito b On z.numnotcre=b.numnotcre
 inner join MInventario c On c.coditems=z.coditems
 inner join MClientes d On d.codclien=b.codclien   
 where b.fechanot between  '09/01/2019' and '09/03/2019'  and b.statnc=3  AND b.codmedico='333' and z.coditems  not in ( 'CMKCINTRON','CMKCINT1CO','CMKCINTSEG' ,'0000000000')
 order by numfactu desc

SELECT sum(a.subtotal) subtotal, SUM(a.descuento) descuento,0 impuesto, 0 envio, sum(a.total) total from cma_MFactura a  inner join MClientes b On a.codclien=b.codclien  where a.fechafac between '09/03/2019' and '09/03/2019' and a.codmedico='333' and a.statfact=3 and a.numfactu in (select distinct numfactu from cma_DFactura a where  a.fechafac between '09/03/2019' and '09/03/2019' and a.cod_subgrupo in('CEL MADRE','INTRAVENOSO','TERAPIA LASER') and a.coditems in( select b.coditems from exclusivos b where b.Codmedico='333'  ))
